 Let's know how to avoid this problem and its side effects during pregnancy
 
 
 - thyroid se nijaat paane ke liye uskasahi ilaaj jaruri heisaliye garbhvatee mahila ko garbhavastha ke dauraan har maheene thyroid kii jaanch karwaani chahie

 haal hi main aae ucch nyaayalay ke ek faisle main khanan rishwatakhori maamle main yediurppa ko bari kar die jane ke baad bhaajapa par unhen dobaaraa mukhyamantri banane kaa dabaav bad rahaa he
 Former Chief Minister Yeddyurappa has said that he has the support of 70 members out of 120 members of BJP in the 225-member assembly
 inamen ek namankit sadsy bhi shaamil he
 Yeddyurappa and his supporters, including several ministers, are meeting in a resort on the outskirts of Bangalore to decide whether they should boycott the assembly to meet their demands from the central leadership
 dilli main kareeb 10 bhaajapa saansad kendriya netritv par gauda ke sthaan par yediurppa kii niyukti ke liye dabaav bana rahe hai
 Senior party leader Arun Jaitley told reporters that he is in touch with Yeddyurappa and he hopes to find a solution to the crisis
 tippaniyan On 31 July last year, Yeddyurappa was removed from the post of Chief Minister by putting pressure on him
 rajya ke tatkaaleen lokayukta ne apni jaanch main paaya tha ki yediurppa ke parivaar ke sadasyon ne do khanan companiyon kaa paksh lene ke evaj main unase kareeb 30 karod rupee liye the
 After this Yeddyurappa had to step down from the post of Chief Minister
 unke sthaan par chaar agast ko gauda ne mukhyamantri pad sambhala tha lekin yediurppa jaldi hi unka virodh karne lage or khud kii dobaaraa niyukti ke liye dabaav banane lage
 After this, in the High Court judgment on March 7, the demand for making him Chief Minister increased after the Lokayukta report and the case registered against Yeddyurappa were invalidated
 sabaki nazren is baat par tiki he ki yediurppa ke samarthak satr kaa bahishkaar kar centre kii mushkilen kitni badhaate hai or centre kaa is par kya rukh rahata he
 BJP President Nitin Gadkari, meanwhile, said in Mumbai that the party's top leadership, after talking to Yeddyurappa, was trying to resolve the renewed leadership dispute in Karnataka
 gadakari ne bharosa jataayaa ki yediurppa aisa kuch bhi nahin karenge, jisase party kii chhavi dhoomil ho
 Speaking to reporters, Gadkari said, "on the recommendation of the Lokayukta, we asked Yeddyurappa to resign
 ham unase baatcheet kar rahe hai
 He is a good party worker
 " Yeddyurappa, the architect of the ongoing crisis in the ruling BJP in Karnataka, has given 48 hours to the party leadership on Sunday
 is bare main gadakari ne kaha, "yediurppa aisa kuch bhi nahin karenge, jisase party kii chhavi dhoomil ho
 They should wait for the party's decision
 ham is bare main jald nirnay lene ko patibaddh hai
 "he said," our conversation is going on
 bhaajapa loktantric party he
 We will consider it and decide when the appropriate time comes
 " Karnataka Chief Minister DV Sadananda Gowda is scheduled to present the budget on Wednesday, but given Yeddyurappa's stance, it is clear that he does not want Gowda to present the budget
 ravivaar shaam patrakaron se yediurppa ne kaha tha, "aap 48 ghante pratiksha kariye, aapako jaankaree ho jaaegi
 " apane awaas par 50 se adhik vidhayakon ke saath baithak ke baad yediurppa ne kaha, "party ke 120 vidhayakon main se 70 kaa samarthan mere paas he
 We are gathering at one place so that the party leadership knows the situation and the leadership takes the right decision soon
 " Yeddyurappa took the 55 mlas of the party to a place outside Bengaluru by two buses
 vidhayakon ko le jate samay unhone kaha, "yahaan 55 vidhayak hai
 15 more mlas will come here tomorrow
 " It is to be known that the Minister of Rural Development Jagdish Shettar, who once defended Yeddyurappa, has come in his support

 tippaniyan On 31 July last year, Yeddyurappa was removed from the post of Chief Minister by putting pressure on him

 bhaajapa ke adhyaksh nitin gadakari ne mumbai main is bich kaha ki party kaa sheersh netritv yediurppa se baatcheet kar karnataka main nae sire se uthe netritv vivaad ko sulajhane kaa prayaas kar rahaa he
 Gadkari expressed confidence that Yeddyurappa would not do anything that would tarnish the party's image
 gadakari ne patrakaron se baatcheet main kaha, "lokayukta kii sifarish par hamane yediurppa se istipha dene ko kaha tha
 We are talking to them
 vah party ke achche kaaryakarta hai
 " karnataka main sattarudh bhaajapa main netritv ko lekar chal rahe maujuuda sankat ke sutaradhar yediurppa ne ravivaar ko party netritv ko 48 ghante kaa samay diya he
 About this, Gadkari said, "yeddyurappa will not do anything that tarnishes the image of the party
 unhen party ke faisle kaa intjaar karnaa chahie
 We are committed to take a quick decision in this regard
 " unhone kaha, "hamaari baatcheet chal rahi he
 The BJP is a democratic party
 ham is par vichaar karenge or upyukt samay aane par nirnay lenge
 " karnataka ke mukhyamantri divi sadanand gauda buudhvaar ko bajet pesh karne vaale hai lekin yediurppa ke rukh ko dekhte hue spasht he ki vah nahin chaahate ki gauda bajet pesh karen
 Yeddyurappa told reporters on Sunday evening, "you wait for 48 hours, you will know
 " After meeting with more than 50 mlas at his residence, Yeddyurappa said, ‚ÄúI have the support of 70 of the 120 mlas of the party
 ham ek sthaan par ikattha ho rahe hai taaki party netritv ko sthiti ko pataa chale or netritv sheeghra sahi nirnay le
 " yediurppa party ke 55 vidhayakon ko do bason se bengaluru ke baahar ek sthaan par le gaye
 While carrying the mlas, he said, ‚Äúthere are 55 mlas here
 15 or vidhayak kal yahaan aa jaaenge
 " gyaat ho ki kabhi yediurppa kii khilaafat karne vaale gramin vikaas mantri jagadish shettar unke samarthan main aa gaye hai
 Yeddyurappa relinquished the post of Chief Minister on 31 July last year on corruption charges
 iske baad gauda chaar agast ko mukhyamantri bane
 After a recent High Court verdict acquitted Yeddyurappa in the mining bribery case, the BJP is under increasing pressure to make him the chief minister again
 purv mukhyamantri yediurppa ne 225 sadasyeey vidhansabha ke bhaajapa ke 120 sadasyon main se unhen 70 sadasyon kaa samarthan praapt hone kii baat kahi he
 They also include a nominated member
 yediurppa va kai mantriyon sahit unke samarthak bengaluru ke bahari ilaake main ek resort main baithak kar yah tay kar rahe hai ki kya unhen kendriya netritv se apni maang manwaane ke liye vidhansabha kaa bahishkaar karnaa chahie
 About 10 BJP mps in Delhi are pressurizing the central leadership to appoint Yeddyurappa in place of Gowda
 party ke varisht netaa arun jetali ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki vah yediurppa ke sampark main hai or unhen sankat kaa samaadhaan nikalne kii ummid he
 The comments pichley saal 31 july ko yediurppa par dabaav banaakar unhen mukhyamantri pad se hataa diya gaya tha
 The then Lokayukta of the state had found in his investigation that Yeddyurappa's family members had taken nearly Rs 30 crore from him in favor of the two mining companies
 iske baad yediurppa ko mukhyamantri pad se hatana padaa
 In his place, Gowda took over as chief minister on August 4, but Yeddyurappa soon started opposing him and pressing for his own reappointment

 ) Now the biggest bubble cryptocurrency after internet is proving bitcoin
 is vakt 1

 iske aakaar ko samajhane ke liye yah dekhie ki 1 disambar ko prachlan main maujuud rupayon kaa kul mulya takreeban 252 arab (65 ru
 Of 1 dollar)
 janvari 2017 main bitcoin kii kharid-farokht 1,000 dollar se kam par kii ja rahi thi or disambar ke pehle pakhwaade main yah 16,000 dollar par pahunch gaya
 This increase in price by 2,000 per cent led to a huge increase in its business
 ab kai hindustani isamen jute gaye hai or kai share bazaar bhi rupye main bitcoin kaa kaarobaar hone de rahe hai
 The price of bitcoin keeps on fluctuating: 20% change in a single session is common
 isaki tulana main sone kii keemat main puure saal takreeban 8 fisadi kaa badlaav aayaa
 This fluctuation makes it extremely risky
 aaj aap ek bitcoin main ek car kharid sakate hai, agle hafte ho saktaa he, do kaaren kharid len yaa phir mahaj ek dopahiyaa bhar
 So if you are dealing in bitcoin, it would be unwise to put your entire amount at stake in it
 isliye thodaa-thodaa khelen
 Bitcoin Unique Computer Code is fought for novices
 nae bitcoin ganit ke sawaalon ko hal karke banaae (nikaale) jate hai
 Each coin can be divided into 100 million unique pieces called 'satoshi'
 iskaa yah naam iske mashhoor avishkaarak satoshi naakamoto ke sakvamaan main rakhaa gaya he
 Bitcoins are created with clever cryptography
 isamen ek khule, baante gaye, electronic khate kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he, jise 'blockchen' kaha jaataa he jisamen samay kii mohar lage lenden ke 'block' hote hai
 After it is created, every transaction in bitcoin is continuously recorded in the blockchain
 blockchen kii prati koi bhi downlod kar saktaa he or coin ke lenden kaa itihaas dekh saktaa he
 Bitcoins are kept in a digital wallet
 harek wolet kii ek saarvajanik aaidi sankhya yaa saarvajanik chaabi hoti he
 Each wallet also has a private key that only its owner knows
 agar yah chaabi gum jaae to isamen rakhe coin gaayab ho jaaenge or unhen waapas hasil karne kaa koi tarika nahin he
 Transactions are done using this private key with that public account number so that the 'fixed coin' can be inserted into another wallet
 harek lenden ek khaas 'hesh' (encripted) messej yaa sandesh taiyaar karata he jiske saath chhedchhad nahin kii ja sakati
 Anyone can test this message by applying public key
 jab lenden kaa sandesh bhej diya jaataa he, to yujar aasaani se jaanch kar saktaa he ki (i) wolet main ve nishchit coin vaaki hai yaa nahin or (ii) ek hi coin se do lenden karke koi dhokhadhadi to nahin ho rahi he
 When most users test the authenticity of the transaction, the blockchain is updated by adding that transaction to a new 'block'
 ek lenden kii tasdik karne main 10 minute lagate hai
 Cryptocurrency exchanges make bitcoin transactions possible in many currencies
 ye exange us wolet kaa logon yaa sansthaaon se milan karte hue kevaisi kii maang karenge
 But transactions outside the exchange are easy
 ek nayaa wolet banaaen, isamen coin rakhen or nakadi ke liye nijee chaabi kii adla-badali karen
 Transacting bitcoins in multiple currencies anonymously is an easy way to send cross-border amounts
 keval japan, australia tathaa kuch or desh ise mudra ke taur par manyata dete hai

 Mahatma Gandhi may not have been welcomed in Britain at the time of India's independence movement, but now he has a statue in Parliament Square in London, the capital of this country
 yah pratimaa britain ke purv pradhanmantri winston churchill ke thik bagal main lagaai he, jinhone unhen kabhi 'andhananga fakir' kii sangya di thi
 This nine feet tall bronze statue of Mahatma Gandhi was unveiled by Finance Minister Arun Jaitley
 is maukey par british pradhanmantri david camran bhi maujuud the
 Apart from these, Bollywood superstar Amitabh Bachchan and Gandhi's grandson Gopal Krishna Gandhi were also present in London on this occasion

 The installation of the Mahatma Gandhi statue was announced last year
 gandhi pehle bhartiya or kabhi bhi kisi pad par naa rahe aise pehle vyakti hai jinaki murti yahaan lagaayi gayi he
 On this occasion, Cameron said, 'this statue is a magnificent tribute to one of the greatest personalities of world politics and by placing a statue of Mahatma Gandhi on this famous square, we are giving him an eternal place in our country
 ‚Äô gandhi ke kuch prasiddh shabdon kaa ullekh karte hue camran ne kaha ki gandhi kii shikshaayen aaj bhi praasangik hai
 He said, 'this statue symbolizes the amazing special friendship between the world's oldest and largest democracy as well as the global strength of Gandhi's messages
 ‚Äô The British Prime Minister said, 'our relations with India have always remained close and they continue to grow with mutual respect, cooperation and trade with equality and undoubtedly through the 1
5 million Indians living in the UK who served in that UK Has contributed greatly to the construction that it is today, and has brought the two countries closer to their benefit
 ‚Äô Jaitley, who was specially invited to the UK for the unveiling of the statue, said it symbolized the spirit of British courtesy that he had now honored a man who was traditionally considered his antagonist
 jetali ne kaha, ‚Äòyah britain kii udaartaa or british loktantr kaa ek mahaan yogadan he ki unhone ab gandhi ko is desh ke sabase mahatvapurn saarvajanik sthal par jagah di he

 ‚Äô unhone kaha, ‚Äòyah pratimaa yah sunishchit karne main madad karegi ki aane vaali pidiyon ke liye gandhi kii viraasat jinda rahe
 It is an important, historic moment celebrating the strong ties between the two countries
 bharat or britain ek jaise mulya saajha karte hai or hamaare bich ek barabari kii bhagidaari he

 After the partition of Bihar in November 2000, 54 out of 61 cases in this regard were transferred to Jharkhand
 sibiai kii vibhinn adaalaton ne 43 se adhik maamalon main faisla suna diya he
 Lalu Prasad and Jagannath Mishra were accused in five cases
 is bich, padosi rajya bihar main prashasan ne is faisle ke maddenjar somvaar ko chetavanee jari kar di he
 The state administration had already issued a warning in view of the apprehension of the performance of RJD supporters
 tippaniyan a police officer said, "the Police Headquarters has instructed all the Superintendents of Police to remain alert and have kept a close watch after the decision on Lalu Prasad in the fodder scam case
 " According to the police, an alert was issued after secret information about supporters of RJD leaders and activists, including RJD, was protesting on the streets amidst the possibility of a verdict against Lalu
 " unhone bataaya ki hinsa paidaa karne kii koshish kii padtaal or is par niyantran lagane ke liye samvedansheel ilaakon main atirikt surakshakarmi tainaat kiye gaye hai
 After the partition of Bihar in the year 2000, Chaibasa district has come to Jharkhand
 isliye chaara ghotaalaa se jude kuch maamle navgathit rajya jharkhand kii nichali adaalat ko sthanantarit ho gaye
 Lalu Prasad arrived in Ranchi on Sunday with son Tejashwi by plane and stayed in the guest house of the railway
 somvaar ko nyaayalay jane ke dauraan unhone ranchi ke ratu road sthit durga mandir main prarthana kii
 Several RJD leaders, including mps Raghuvansh Prasad Singh, Prabhunath Singh and Lalu's brother-in-law Sadhu Yadav, were present in the judging room at the time of the verdict
 idhar, daagi va sajayaftaa saansadon va vidhayakon kaa bachaav karne vaale centre sarkaar ke adhyadesh ko congress ke upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi dwaara bakawaas qaraar dene ke baad lalu prasad or unke bhavishya ke liye yah faisla mahatvapurn ho gaya he
 There is a possibility that this ordinance may be withdrawn
 is adhyadesh ke anusaar doshi saansadon evam vidhayakon ko ayogy nahin tehraaya jayega
 56 people were charged in the case, but seven accused died during the trial, two became public witnesses, one confessed to the crime and one was acquitted of the charge
 nyaayadhish pravaas kumaar singh ne 15 july ko faisle kaa din mukarrar kiya tha or 45 shesh aropiyon se adaalat main pesh hone ke liye kaha tha
 Lalu Prasad took refuge in the Jharkhand High Court and then the Supreme Court and appealed for a change of judge in the case
 donon nyaayalayon ne is apil ko khaarij kar diya tha or unhen sibiai kii vishesh adaalat main sunwaayee puri karne ke nirdesh die gaye the
 He resigned as Chief Minister in 1997 after Lalu Prasad was named in the CBI investigation of this scam in 1996
 november 2000 main bihar ke vibhaajan ke baad is sambandh main 61 main se 54 maamle jharkhand sthanantarit kar die gaye the
 Various CBI courts have pronounced judgment in more than 43 cases
 lalu prasad or jagannatha mishra ko paanch maamalon main aaropee banaaya gaya tha
 Meanwhile, the administration in the neighboring state of Bihar has issued a warning on Monday in view of this decision
 rajya prashasan ne rajd samarthakon ke pradarshan kii ashanka ko dekhte hue pehle se hi chetavanee jari kar diya tha
 The comments ek police adhikari ne kaha, "police mukhyalay ne sabhi police adhikshakon ko alert rahane ke nirdesh dete hue chaara ghotaalaa maamle main lalu prasad par faisla aane ke baad kareebi nigaah banaae rakhane kii maang kii he
 " police ke anusaar, lalu ke khilaaf faisla aane kii sambhaavna ke bich rajd netaaon or kaaryakartaaon sahit samarthakon ke sadakon par pradarshan karne kii gupt jaankaree milane par alert jari kar diya gaya
 "he said that additional security personnel have been deployed in sensitive areas to investigate and try to create violence
 lalu prasad ravivaar ko putr tejasvi ke saath vimaan se ranchi pahunche the or railway ke atithi grih main tehre the
 On Monday while going to court, he prayed at the Durga temple on Ratu Road, Ranchi
 saansad raghuvansh prasad singh, prabhunath singh or lalu ke saale sadhu yadav sahit kai rajd netaa faisle ke vakt nyaay kaksh main maujuud the
 Here, this decision has become important for Lalu Prasad and his future after Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi called the Central Government Ordinance defending tainted and convicted mps and mlas
 aisi sambhaavna he ki is adhyadesh ko waapas liya ja saktaa he
 According to this ordinance, convicted mps and mlas will not be disqualified
 is maamle main 56 logon ko aaropee banaaya gaya tha, lekin sunwaayee ke dauraan saat aropiyon kii maut ho gai, do sarkari gavaah ban gaye, ek ne aparaadh kabool kar liya or ek ko aarope se mukt kar diya gaya
 Judge Pravas Kumar Singh set the verdict on July 15 and asked the 45 remaining accused to appear in the court
 lalu prasad ne jharkhand ucch nyaayalay or iske baad sarvocch nyaayalay kii sharan lee thi or is maamle main nyaayadhish badale jane kii apil kii thi
